<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Gorelov_youri_g_pacifist.jpg/220px-Gorelov_youri_g_pacifist.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="248" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Gorelov_youri_g_pacifist.jpg/330px-Gorelov_youri_g_pacifist.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Gorelov_youri_g_pacifist.jpg/440px-Gorelov_youri_g_pacifist.jpg 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="1015" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:портянка.html>портя́нки</a> (1)</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портянка.html>портя́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">portjánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портянка.html>портя́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портянка.html>портя́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портянка.html>портя́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> footwrap, portyanki <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a strip of cloth worn around the feet</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Russia or Russians</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a person trusting the government, believing any propaganda, following leaders</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an over-patriotic Russian/Soviet citizen</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совок.html>сово́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sovók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватник.html>ва́тник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vátnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***поручение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a> (4402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручать.html>поруча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poručátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to commission, to entrust</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ручать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ručatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to vouch, to guarantee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ruká</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see there for more)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poručénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>assignment, commission, errand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломатический.html>дипломати́ческое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">diplomatíčeskoje <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">diplomatic mission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to charge; to instruct</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ vážnoje <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">charge with an important mission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on dal jej éto <b>poručénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he gave her the commission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́нию</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>poručéniju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the instructions; on a commission; on behalf; per procurationem</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посо́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:особый.html>осо́бым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ниям</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posól po osóbym <b>poručénijam</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ambassador at large</span></div></dd></dl></li>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> словообразования: порученье.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-поруч-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ениj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***поручиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́ться</a> (12072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручить.html>поручи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poručítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poručítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warrant, to guarantee, to certify, to answer for, to vouch for <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>poručílsja</b> za éto golovój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>answered/vouched</b> for it with my life; I staked my life on it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручу́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> ....</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>Poručúsʹ</b> za to, što ....</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>will guarantee</b> that ....</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ručátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручаться.html>поруча́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poručátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to assure, to promise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́лся</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лаю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>poručílsja</b>, što sdélaju éto.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I promised I will do it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bet, to be sure</li>

***порхать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порхать.html>порха́ть</a> (14606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pьrxati</i>/<i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pъrxati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порхать.html>порха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порхну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flit, to flutter, to fly about</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hop, to move <i>(from place to place)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порхать.html>порха́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одного́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́е</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>porxátʹ</b> s odnovó mesta rabóty na drugóje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to job-hop</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a> (12865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портить.html>по́ртить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pórtitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spoil, damage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pórča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рчи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рчи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spoiling</li>
<li>damage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груз.html>гру́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pórča</b> grúza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cargo damage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pórča</b> továra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">spoilage, damage of goods</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>corruption
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порча.html>по́рча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нных</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pórča</b> dánnyx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">data corruption</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>evil curse, hex
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:портить.html>по́рчу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">navodítʹ pórču</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put an evil curse; to hex</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">порыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
